It is played with black and white stones on a 15x15 intersections board. Stones can not be moved or removed from the board once placed. The winner is the first player to get an unbroken row of five stones horizontally, vertically, or diagonally.\r\n\r\nThe Gomoku Pro rule set some restrictions on the first few moves to reduce the advantage Black has by going first:\r\n1.
